    @staticmethod
    def merge(left, right):
        """ Merge helper
            Complexity: O(n)
        """
        arr = []
        left_cursor, right_cursor = 0, 0
        while left_cursor < len(left) and right_cursor < len(right):
            # Sort each one and place into the result
            if left[left_cursor] <= right[right_cursor]:
